  • paraview._colorMaps

Source code for paraview._colorMaps

r"""
This is a deprecated module and should not be used anymore.
These are legacy colormap XMLs kept around till `paraview.lookuptable` module is deprecated
and removed."""

__colorMapsXML = """
<ColorMaps>
  <!-- ParaView Default Color Maps -->
  <ColorMap name="Cool to Warm" space="Diverging">
    <Point x="0.0" r="0.23137254902" g="0.298039215686" b="0.752941176471" o="0.0"/>
    <Point x="0.5" r="0.865" g="0.865" b="0.865" o="0.0"/>
    <Point x="1.0" r="0.705882352941" g="0.0156862745098" b="0.149019607843" o="1.0"/>
    <NaN r="1.0" g="1.0" b="0.0"/>
  </ColorMap>
  <ColorMap name="Blue to Red Rainbow" space="HSV">
    <Point x="0.0" r="0.0" g="0.0" b="1.0" o="0.0"/>
    <Point x="1.0" r="1.0" g="0.0" b="0.0" o="0.0"/>
    <NaN r="0.498039215686" g="0.498039215686" b="0.498039215686"/>
  </ColorMap>
  <ColorMap name="Red to Blue Rainbow" space="HSV">
    <Point x="0.0" r="1.0" g="0.0" b="0.0" o="0.0"/>
    <Point x="1.0" r="0.0" g="0.0" b="1.0" o="1.0"/>
    <NaN r="0.498039215686" g="0.498039215686" b="0.498039215686"/>
  </ColorMap>

[docs]def getColorMaps():
    """Returns the vtkPVXMLElement instance for the default (legacy) color maps"""
    global __colorMapsXML
    from paraview.modules.vtkPVCore import vtkPVXMLParser
    parser = vtkPVXMLParser()
    if parser.Parse(__colorMapsXML):
        return parser.GetRootElement()
    return None
